DStfYds	Defensive Stuff Yards	Yards lost on defensive stuffs. For players, the total yards are split for an assisted tackle.	
player: ((-1)*sum(event.playYardsGained) HAVING event.tackle and opponent.event.rush and event.playTypePrecise != 'Kneel' and opponent.event.playYardsGained <= 0) - (0.5*sum(event.playYardsGained) HAVING event.assist and opponent.event.rush and event.playTypePrecise != 'Kneel' and opponent.event.playYardsGained <= 0)
team: (-1)*sum(event.playYardsGained) HAVING opponent.event.rush and event.playTypePrecise != 'Kneel' and opponent.event.playYardsGained <= 0
defense	aggregate
DStuffs	Defensive Stuffs	Solo or assisted tackles on any rushing play that results in no gain or a loss of yardage. For players, a solo tackle is worth a full stuff and an assisted tackle is worth half a stuff for each player.	
player: (count(event.tackle) + count(event.assist)/2) having opponent.event.rush and event.playTypePrecise != 'Kneel' and opponent.event.playYardsGained <= 0
team: count(event.play) HAVING event.play and opponent.event.rush and event.playTypePrecise != 'Kneel' and opponent.event.playYardsGained <= 0
defense	aggregate
